<t>CREATE TABLE game (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    release_date DATE,
    platform VARCHAR(100)
);

CREATE TABLE player (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    registration_date DATE
);

CREATE TABLE developer (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    founded_date DATE,
    headquarters VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE review (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    game_id INT,
    player_id INT,
    rating DECIMAL(2, 1),
    review_text TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES game(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES player(id)
);</t><s>INSERT INTO game (id, title, release_date, platform) VALUES (1, 'Game of Thrones', '2021-05-15', 'PC') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE title = 'Game of Thrones', release_date = '2021-05-15', platform = 'PC';</s>

    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    founded_date DATE,
    headquarters VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE game (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    release_date DATE,
    platform VARCHAR(100)
);

CREATE TABLE player (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    registration_date DATE
);</t><s>INSERT INTO game (id, title, release_date, platform) VALUES (1, 'Game of Thrones', '2021-05-15', 'PC') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE title = 'Game of Thrones', release_date = '2021-05-15', platform = 'PC';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE review (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    game_id INT,
    player_id INT,
    rating DECIMAL(2, 1),
    review_text TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES game(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES player(id)
);

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>UPSERT INTO players (player_id, player_name, player_level, player_score) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 10, 500) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE player_level = 10, player_score = 500;</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE players (player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), player_level INT, player_score INT);

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>upsert into players (player_id, player_name, player_level, player_score) values (1, 'john doe', 10, 500) on duplicate key update player_level = 10, player_score = 500;</s>

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));</t><s>UPSERT INTO players (player_id, player_name, player_level, player_score) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 10, 500) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE player_level = 10, player_score = 500;</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));

CREATE TABLE players (player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), player_level INT, player_score INT);</t><s>upsert into games (game_id, game_name, game_genre, game_release_date) values (1, 'game a', 'action', '2022-01-15') on duplicate key update game_genre = 'action';</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>upsert into games (game_id, game_name, game_genre, game_release_date) values (1, 'game a', 'action', '2022-01-15') on duplicate key update game_genre = 'action';</s>

CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>UPSERT INTO achievements (achievement_id, achievement_name, player_id, achievement_date) VALUES (1, 'First Achievement', 1, '2022-01-20') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE achievement_date = '2022-01-20';</s>

CREATE TABLE achievements (achievement_id INT PRIMARY KEY, achievement_name VARCHAR(255), player_id INT, achievement_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));</t><s>upsert into achievements (achievement_id, achievement_name, player_id, achievement_date) values (1, 'first achievement', 1, '2022-01-20') on duplicate key update achievement_date = '2022-01-20';</s>

CREATE TABLE games (game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_name VARCHAR(255), game_genre VARCHAR(255), game_release_date DATE);</t><s>upsert into achievements (achievement_id, achievement_name, player_id, achievement_date) values (1, 'first achievement', 1, '2022-01-20') on duplicate key update achievement_date = '2022-01-20';</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));

CREATE TABLE user_ratings (rating_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, rating FLOAT, rating_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id));

CREATE TABLE games (game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_name VARCHAR(255), game_genre VARCHAR(255), game_release_date DATE);
